Heard about this local spot from some friends who swear by the food, so had to give it a try.

This review is based off the brisket burger and service, maybe some of the other menu items are better.

First the service:
There were a few customers already waiting when I placed my order so I expected a bit of a wait, but 35 minutes is more than I would expect for no line and maybe 3 orders before mine.  One of the employees son ordered after me and kept sticking his unmasked face into the interior and talking, regardless of what their opinion of the health crisis is it's terrible to
look like the business doesn't value their customers health.

The food:
The Brisket was cooked perfectly, tender and still juicy, but the marinade had an overpowering flavor of liquid smoke ruining the natural flavor of the meat.  There was sauce on the sandwich when I was told they only put the sauce on the side.

Overall not great especially considering the $15 price, but they do know their way around a smoker.</text>

<Text>Absolutely the BEST BBQ in Oceanside and North county. I suspected something great was happening on this corner. Every time I passed by there were lots of cars and people with smiling faces. My wife and I have a few rare days without kids where we can have a nice lunch date together and decided to give this place a try. SO glad we did. Everything, and I mean EVERYTHING on the menu is absolutely off the chart delicious and 100% authentic. Everything looked so good that I was faced with the dilemma of what to order. The owner, obviously very experienced with the dumbfounded look on our faces, stepped in and rescued us from our indecision. He generously provided us with some samples of their delicious smoked brisket, burnt ends, ribs and sausage. Normally, I HATE sausage from the grocery store. But, my friends, this is NO ordinary sausage. Made fresh on the spot...it tastes like the choicest, prime cuts of meat. Not like the fillers, cartilage and gristle you'd find elsewhere. <review>Like many people, if you're not from here finding a good mechanic can be a daunting task...

I'm also not one to write reviews, but this place deserves some more negative reviews.

Let me preface this by saying I had a successful experience with Morin Brothers in the past for a valve adjustment. Everything you could want, good service, friendly people, and good communication. I thought, "awesome, I found a great mechanic to take my vehicles to".

Fast forward a few months, and my 4runner blew a head gasket. Forced to have it towed somewhere, I chose Morin brother again because of my initial experience with them.

Well that was a BAD idea. It felt like a completely different shop this time. First off, they were unwilling to explain to me what they found. I already knew it was a blown head gasket, but they continued to charge me $110 just to tell me what I already knew. I completely understand that's a standard diagnostic fee for a mechanic, but at least provide me with some information on what you did? So over the phone I was trying to get more information (like what did you do that was worth $110) and Elaina, was very short on the phone with me. Speaking very quickly and rushing me off the phone. Not willing AT ALL to explain what was going on, what they saw etc. So then I asked what the mechanic saw and she replies "it's a blown head gasket and they just heard some noise from the timing chain". Completely unwilling to explain anything to me.

Then I asked for another day to make a decision. So I called almost every other shop in slo county and found the cost of my repairs to range from $1500-2500 compared to the $4400 Morin quoted me!! I could not believe they would try to charge me that much. They didn't even provide a second option for a new engine or anything else (like most shops would), They just quoted me $4400 and that was it. From rushing me off the phone to the outrageous quote they CLEARLY did not want my business.

THEN I get a call from Jesse asking me if I had made a decision. Which I hadn't yet, and needed a little more time. I was a few hours past the 1 day I had asked for to make my decision. On our phone call I respond with "can I have a little more time" and you say end the conversation with "We could really use the space in our lot" what do you think that communicates to your customer?

The entire experience communicates nothing but "we don't care about you or your business."

So I had my 4runner towed elsewhere and hope others don't make the same mistake I do. Don't waste your time or money here.<//review><Rate>1<//Rate><Pictures>None< /Pictures></record></dataset><record>
